<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">Overview</span></h2>
<dl>
<dd> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/File:Fused_Riddermark_Relics-icon.png" class="image"><img alt="Fused Riddermark Relics-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Fused_Riddermark_Relics-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></a> <strong class="selflink">Relics</strong> are items that can be slotted on <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Legendary_Items" title="Legendary Items">Legendary Items</a> to add additional bonuses to their user. There are five types of relics:
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd><ul>
<li> Settings, which grant will/might/morale/power and tactical and physical mastery
</li>
<li> Gems, which grant vitality/agility/fate and critical rating
</li>
<li> Runes, which grant incoming healing/in-combat morale regen/in-combat power regen and block/parry/evade
</li>
<li> Crafted, which grant might/agility/vitality/will/fate/morale/power/critical rating/tactical mastery/physical mastery
</li>
<li> Mounted relics, which can only be slotted into a bridle, and give a variety of stat bonuses or skill bonuses
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> The first three types also have exceptional versions that are more 
difficult to obtain, and that grant additional or different bonuses.
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> Legendary items have four relic slots (one for each type). Relics 
can be slotted at any time, but slotting a new relic on top of an 
already-slotted relic will destroy the already-slotted relic. The only 
way to unslot relics is to use a <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3ARelic_Removal_Scroll" title="Item:Relic_Removal_Scroll"><span class="ajaxttlink">Relic Removal Scroll</span></a>. 
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd><ul>
<li> <b>NOTE</b> Item levels for Crafted Relics, in this article, refer to the <i>static</i>, not the <i>experience</i>, level.
</li>
<li> <b>IMPORTANT:</b> SSG is constantly tweaking stat values in the 
process of tuning "game balance." These changes are not normally 
announced in the release notes. Therefore, keep in mind that the values 
listed here were correct at the time they were transcribed -- HOWEVER, 
you should always consult the various in-game tables for the latest and 
correct values.
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="How_to_Obtain_Relics">How to Obtain Relics</span></h3>
<dl>
<dd> Relics can be obtained by the following means:
<ul>
<li> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Legendary_Items#Reforging_and_Deconstructing" title="Legendary Items">Deconstructing</a> legendary items (higher level items will yield more and higher tier relics)
</li>
<li> Rare loot from <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Skirmish_Lieutenants" title="Skirmish Lieutenants">Skirmish Lieutenants</a> in <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Skirmish" title="Skirmish">Skirmishes</a>
</li>
<li> Rare loot from <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Skirmish" title="Skirmish">Skirmish</a> end bosses (looted from corpses or from final chests)
</li>
<li> Receiving and deconstructing sealed or <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Fused_Relics" title="Fused Relics">Fused Relics</a> from instances/raid bosses/certain quests/<a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Hobbit_Presents" title="Hobbit Presents">Hobbit Presents</a>
</li>
<li> Barter <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AMark" title="Item:Mark"><span class="ajaxttlink"><img alt="Mark-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Mark-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></span></a> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AMark" title="Item:Mark"><span class="ajaxttlink">Marks</span></a> for fused relics at the <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Skirmish-Legendary_Items" title="Skirmish-Legendary Items">Legendary skirmish vendor</a>.
</li>
<li> Barter <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AMark_of_Victory" title="Item:Mark_of_Victory"><span class="ajaxttlink"><img alt="Mark of Victory-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Mark_of_Victory-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></span></a> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AMark_of_Victory" title="Item:Mark_of_Victory"><span class="ajaxttlink">Marks of Victory</span></a> with <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/R%C3%BAnar" title="Rúnar">Rúnar</a> the Sage of Moria in <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Twenty-first_Hall" title="Twenty-first Hall" class="mw-redirect">Twenty-first Hall</a> for a <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AChest_of_Relics" title="Item:Chest_of_Relics"><span class="ajaxttlink">Chest of Relics</span></a>.
</li>
<li> Barter various regional faction tokens at their respective traders for fused relics.
</li>
<li> Barter <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3ACommendation" title="Item:Commendation"><span class="ajaxttlink"><img alt="Commendation-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Commendation-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></span></a> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3ACommendation" title="Item:Commendation"><span class="ajaxttlink">Commendations</span></a> with various traders in <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Gl%C3%A2n_Vraig" title="Glân Vraig">Glân Vraig</a> in the <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Ettenmoors" title="Ettenmoors">Ettenmoors</a>. (The Relics are NOT class restricted.)
</li>
<li> Barter <span style="font-size: 1em;"><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AKhuzdul_Tablets" title="Item:Khuzdul_Tablets"><span class="ajaxttlink"><img alt="Khuzdul Tablets-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Khuzdul_Tablets-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></span></a></span>&nbsp;<a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AKhuzdul_Tablets" title="Item:Khuzdul Tablets"><span class="ajaxttlink">Khuzdul Tablets</span></a> or <span style="font-size: 1em;"><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3ARusted_Dwarf_Tools" title="Item:Rusted_Dwarf_Tools"><span class="ajaxttlink"><img alt="Rusted Dwarf Tools-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Rusted_Dwarf_Tools-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></span></a></span>&nbsp;<a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3ARusted_Dwarf_Tools" title="Item:Rusted Dwarf Tools"><span class="ajaxttlink">Rusted Dwarf Tools</span></a> for <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relics#Tier_1_Relics" title="Relics">Tier 1 Relics</a> with legendary class traders at <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Imlad_Lalaith" title="Imlad Lalaith">Imlad Lalaith</a>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tiers_and_Relic_Forging">Tiers and Relic Forging</span></h3>
<dl>
<dd> Relics are divided into ten tiers, with higher tier relics delivering improved buffs when slotted in your Legendary Item.
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> For a fee, either with silver (the default) or with <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AShard" title="Item:Shard"><span class="ajaxttlink">shards</span></a>, relics can be <b>forged</b> by a <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic-master" title="Relic-master">Relic-master</a> to combine lower-tier relics into higher-tier relics. 
<dl>
<dd> (Currency selection is found at the bottom of the Relic-master's panel).
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> You can select which relics to combine by using the increment 
arrows and then clicking the "Combine" button, or use the "Auto Combine"
 button for a random selection of relics.
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> The normal result of Relic Forging will be one or two relics of the next higher tier and possibly relic shards.
</dd>
<dd> Occasionally the forging may complete with a critical success, 
which will yield 2 or more relics of one or more higher tiers and/or 
relic shards.  
</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd> The following table shows the number of relics needed to to forge each higher tier (assuming no critical forges).
<dl>
<dd> Tier 1 relics are obtained by deconstructing LIs of other Classes, i.e. those which your character cannot use.
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Refining">Refining</span></h3>
<dl>
<dd>Relics can be refined into <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Item%3AShard" title="Item:Shard"><span class="ajaxttlink">shards</span></a> which are used for melding or instead of silver to perform legendary services. There's a small chance to receive <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Heritage_Runes" title="Heritage Runes">Heritage Runes</a> upon refining.  Speak to a <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic-master" title="Relic-master">Relic-master</a> to refine.
</dd>
</dl>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Melding">Melding</span></h3>
<p>Melding combines shards into legendary items, legacies, scrolls, or with relics to create new relics.  Speak to a <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic-master" title="Relic-master">Relic-master</a> to meld.
</p>

<td><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic:Insignia_of_Soothing" title="Relic:Insignia of Soothing">Insignia of Soothing</a></td>
<td align="center"> 65 </td>
<td> -10% Song of Soothing Incoming Healing Debuff </td>
<td> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Bellflower_Pitts" title="Bellflower Pitts">Bellflower Pitts</a> </td>
<td> Minstrel
</td></tr>
<tr class="even">
<td> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/File:Rune-keeper_Relic-icon.png" class="image"><img alt="Rune-keeper Relic-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Rune-keeper_Relic-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></a></td>
<td><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic:Insignia_of_the_Tirade" title="Relic:Insignia of the Tirade">Insignia of the Tirade</a></td>
<td align="center"> 65 </td>
<td> +10% Ceaseless Argument Slow Chance </td>
<td> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Telemnar" title="Telemnar">Telemnar</a> </td>
<td> Rune-keeper
</td></tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/File:Warden_Relic-icon.png" class="image"><img alt="Warden Relic-icon.png" src="Relics%20-%20Lotro-Wiki.com_files/Warden_Relic-icon.png" width="32" height="32"></a></td>
<td><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Relic:Insignia_of_the_Boar" title="Relic:Insignia of the Boar">Insignia of the Boar</a></td>
<td align="center"> 65 </td>
<td> +15% Boar's Rush Daze chance on hit </td>
<td> <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Landru" title="Landru">Landru</a> </td>
<td> Warden
</td></tr>
</tbody></table></dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>All these barterers are located at <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Gl%C3%A2n_Vraig" title="Glân Vraig">Glân Vraig</a> in the <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Ettenmoors" title="Ettenmoors">Ettenmoors</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Retired_Relics_Index">Retired Relics Index</span></h2>
<p><a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Retired_Relics" title="Retired Relics">Retired Relics</a>: An index that contains the information of relics before <a href="http://lotro-wiki.com/index.php/Patch_Notes_-_Update_2_Echoes_of_The_Dead" title="Patch Notes - Update 2 Echoes of The Dead">Update 2 Echoes of The Dead</a>. While these relics can no longer be obtained in game, any relics that existed before the patch remain on an individual basis.
</p>
